SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "DIRECTIONAL" "SHADOWS_OFF" "LIGHTMAP_OFF" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" }
"!!GLES


#ifdef VERTEX

attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
attribute vec4 _glesTANGENT;
uniform highp vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform lowp vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform highp vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 _Object2World;
uniform highp mat4 _World2Object;
uniform highp vec4 unity_Scale;
uniform highp vec4 _MainTex_ST;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying lowp vec4 xlv_COLOR0;
varying lowp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
varying lowp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD3;
void main ()
{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize(_glesTANGENT.xyz);
  tmpvar_1.w = _glesTANGENT.w;
  vec3 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = normalize(_glesNormal);
  highp vec3 shlight_3;
  lowp vec3 tmpvar_4;
  lowp vec3 tmpvar_5;
  mat3 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6[0] = _Object2World[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_6[1] = _Object2World[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_6[2] = _Object2World[2].xyz;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_7;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_7 = tmpvar_1.xyz;
  tmpvar_8 = (((tmpvar_2.yzx * tmpvar_1.zxy) - (tmpvar_2.zxy * tmpvar_1.yzx)) * _glesTANGENT.w);
  highp mat3 tmpvar_9;

SubProgram "glesdesktop " {
Keywords { "DIRECTIONAL" "SHADOWS_OFF" "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" }

attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord1;

{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize(_glesTANGENT.xyz);
  tmpvar_1.w = _glesTANGENT.w;

  tmpvar_5[0].x = tmpvar_3.x;
  tmpvar_5[0].y = tmpvar_4.x;
  tmpvar_5[0].z = tmpvar_2.x;
  tmpvar_5[1].x = tmpvar_3.y;
  tmpvar_5[1].y = tmpvar_4.y;
  tmpvar_5[1].z = tmpvar_2.y;
  tmpvar_5[2].x = tmpvar_3.z;
  tmpvar_5[2].y = tmpvar_4.z;
  tmpvar_5[2].z = tmpvar_2.z;

  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;

{

SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 25 math
Keywords { "DIRECTIONAL" "SHADOWS_SCREEN" "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_ON" }

"!!ARBvp1.0

		state.matrix.mvp,
		program.local[5..18] };

TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
MOV R0.xyz, vertex.attrib[14];
MUL R1.xyz, vertex.normal.zxyw, R0.yzxw;
MAD R0.xyz, vertex.normal.yzxw, R0.zxyw, -R1;

		state.matrix.mvp,
		program.local[5..31] };

TEMP R3;
TEMP R4;

DP4 R0.x, vertex.position, c[6];

MAD R1, R0, R0, R1;

RSQ R1.y, R1.y;
RSQ R1.w, R1.w;
RSQ R1.z, R1.z;
MUL R0, R0, R1;
ADD R1, R2, c[0].x;
RCP R1.x, R1.x;
RCP R1.y, R1.y;
RCP R1.w, R1.w;
RCP R1.z, R1.z;
MAX R0, R0, c[0].y;
MUL R0, R0, R1;
MUL R1.xyz, R0.y, c[20];
MAD R1.xyz, R0.x, c[19], R1;
MAD R0.xyz, R0.z, c[21], R1;
MAD R1.xyz, R0.w, c[22], R0;
MUL R0, R4.xyzz, R4.yzzx;
DP4 R3.z, R0, c[28];
DP4 R3.y, R0, c[27];
DP4 R3.x, R0, c[26];
MUL R1.w, R3, R3;
MAD R0.x, R4, R4, -R1.w;

DP4 R2.y, R4, c[24];
DP4 R2.x, R4, c[23];

DP4 R2.z, R0, c[11];
DP4 R2.x, R0, c[9];
DP4 R2.y, R0, c[10];

MOV R1, c[14];

ADD R1, R2, c[0].x;
RCP R1.x, R1.x;
RCP R1.y, R1.y;
RCP R1.w, R1.w;
RCP R1.z, R1.z;

MAD R0.xyz, R0.z, c[22], R1;
MAD R1.xyz, R0.w, c[23], R0;
MUL R0, R4.xyzz, R4.yzzx;
DP4 R3.z, R0, c[29];
DP4 R3.y, R0, c[28];
DP4 R3.x, R0, c[27];

DP4 R2.y, R4, c[25];

 // Stats for Vertex shader:
 //       d3d11 : 30 avg math (23..32)
 //    d3d11_9x : 30 avg math (23..32)
 //        d3d9 : 35 avg math (29..38)
 //      opengl : 32 avg math (26..35)
 // Stats for Fragment shader:
 //       d3d11 : 33 avg math (29..39), 2 avg texture (1..3)
 //    d3d11_9x : 33 avg math (29..39), 2 avg texture (1..3)
 //        d3d9 : 39 avg math (35..45), 2 avg texture (1..3)
 //      opengl : 38 avg math (33..44), 2 avg texture (1..3)
 Pass {
  Name "FORWARD"
  Tags { "LIGHTMODE"="ForwardAdd" }
  ZWrite Off
  Fog {
   Color (0,0,0,0)
  }
  Blend One One
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 34 math
Keywords { "POINT" }
Bind "vertex" Vertex
Bind "color" Color
Bind "normal" Normal
Bind "texcoord" TexCoord0
Bind "tangent" ATTR14
Matrix 5 [_Object2World]
Matrix 9 [_World2Object]
Matrix 13 [_LightMatrix0]
Vector 17 [_WorldSpaceCameraPos]
Vector 18 [_WorldSpaceLightPos0]
Vector 19 [unity_Scale]
Vector 20 [_MainTex_ST]
"!!ARBvp1.0
PARAM c[21] = { { 1 },
		state.matrix.mvp,
		program.local[5..20] };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
TEMP R3;
MOV R1.xyz, c[17];
MOV R1.w, c[0].x;
MOV R0.xyz, vertex.attrib[14];
DP4 R2.z, R1, c[11];
DP4 R2.y, R1, c[10];
DP4 R2.x, R1, c[9];
MAD R2.xyz, R2, c[19].w, -vertex.position;
MUL R1.xyz, vertex.normal.zxyw, R0.yzxw;
MAD R1.xyz, vertex.normal.yzxw, R0.zxyw, -R1;
MOV R0, c[18];
MUL R1.xyz, R1, vertex.attrib[14].w;
DP4 R3.z, R0, c[11];
DP4 R3.x, R0, c[9];
DP4 R3.y, R0, c[10];
MAD R0.xyz, R3, c[19].w, -vertex.position;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].y, R0, R1;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].z, vertex.normal, R0;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].x, R0, vertex.attrib[14];
DP4 R0.w, vertex.position, c[8];
DP4 R0.z, vertex.position, c[7];

SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "SPOT" }

#ifdef VERTEX

attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
attribute vec4 _glesTANGENT;
uniform highp vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform highp vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;

uniform highp mat4 _Object2World;
uniform highp mat4 _World2Object;

{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize(_glesTANGENT.xyz);
  tmpvar_1.w = _glesTANGENT.w;
  vec3 tmpvar_2;

  tmpvar_7[1].y = tmpvar_6.y;
  tmpvar_7[1].z = tmpvar_2.y;
  tmpvar_7[2].x = tmpvar_5.z;
  tmpvar_7[2].y = tmpvar_6.z;
  tmpvar_7[2].z = tmpvar_2.z;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = (tmpvar_7 * (((_World2Object * _WorldSpaceLightPos0).xyz * unity_Scale.w) - _glesVertex.xyz));

SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 44 math, 3 textures
Keywords { "SPOT" }
Vector 0 [_LightColor0]
Vector 1 [_SpecColor]
Float 2 [_Shininess]
SetTexture 0 [_MainTex] 2D 0
SetTexture 1 [_LightTexture0] 2D 1
SetTexture 2 [_LightTextureB0] 2D 2
"!!ARBfp1.0
PARAM c[6] = { program.local[0..3],
		{ 0, 128, 3, 1 },
		{ 2, 0.5 } };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
TEX R2, fragment.texcoord[0], texture[0], 2D;
DP3 R0.z, fragment.texcoord[3], fragment.texcoord[3];
RCP R0.x, fragment.texcoord[3].w;
MAD R0.xy, fragment.texcoord[3], R0.x, c[5].y;
MOV result.color.w, c[4].x;
TEX R0.w, R0, texture[1], 2D;
TEX R1.w, R0.z, texture[2], 2D;
ADD R0.y, R2, -R2.x;
MUL_SAT R0.x, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4].z;
MAD R0.z, R0.x, R0.y, R2.x;
MUL R0.y, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4].z;
SLT R2.y, c[4].x, fragment.texcoord[3].z;
MUL R0.w, R2.y, R0;
MUL R0.w, R0, R1;
ADD_SAT R0.y, R0, -c[5].x;
ADD R0.x, R2.w, -R2.z;
MAD R0.x, R0.y, R0, R2.z;
ADD R1.x, R0, -R0.z;
MAD_SAT R0.y, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4].z, -c[4].w;
MAD R2.x, R0.y, R1, R0.z;
DP3 R0.x, fragment.texcoord[1], fragment.texcoord[1];
RSQ R0.y, R0.x;
DP3 R0.x, fragment.texcoord[2], fragment.texcoord[2];
MUL R1.xyz, R0.y, fragment.texcoord[1];
RSQ R0.x, R0.x;
MAD R0.xyz, R0.x, fragment.texcoord[2], R1;
DP3 R0.y, R0, R0;
ADD R1.x, fragment.color.primary, -R2;
MAD R0.x, fragment.color.primary.y, R1, R2;
RSQ R1.x, R0.y;
MUL R0.z, R1.x, R0;
MOV R0.y, c[4];
MUL R1.x, R0.y, c[2];
MAX R0.y, R0.z, c[4].x;
POW R0.y, R0.y, R1.x;
MUL R2.x, R0.y, R0;
MUL R0.xyz, R0.x, c[0];
MAX R1.x, R1.z, c[4];
MUL R1.xyz, R0, R1.x;
MOV R0.xyz, c[1];
MUL R0.xyz, R0, c[0];
MUL R0.w, R0, c[5].x;
MAD R0.xyz, R0, R2.x, R1;
MUL result.color.xyz, R0, R0.w;
END
# 44 instructions, 3 R-regs
"
}
SubProgram "d3d9 " {
// Stats: 45 math, 3 textures
Keywords { "SPOT" }
Vector 0 [_LightColor0]
Vector 1 [_SpecColor]
Float 2 [_Shininess]
SetTexture 0 [_MainTex] 2D 0
SetTexture 1 [_LightTexture0] 2D 1
SetTexture 2 [_LightTextureB0] 2D 2
"ps_2_0
dcl_2d s0
dcl_2d s1
dcl_2d s2
def c3, 0.00000000, 128.00000000, 3.00000000, -1.00000000
def c4, 3.00000000, -2.00000000, 0.00000000, 1.00000000
def c5, 0.50000000, 2.00000000, 0, 0
dcl t0.xy
dcl v0.xyzw
dcl t1.xyz
dcl t2.xyz
dcl t3
dp3 r0.x, t3, t3
mov r2.xy, r0.x
rcp r1.x, t3.w
mad r1.xy, t3, r1.x, c5.x
mul_sat r3.x, v0.w, c3.z
texld r0, r1, s1
texld r5, r2, s2
texld r1, t0, s0
add r4.x, r1.y, -r1
mad r1.x, r3, r4, r1
add r2.x, r1.w, -r1.z
mad_sat r0.x, v0.w, c4, c4.y
mad r0.x, r0, r2, r1.z
dp3_pp r2.x, t1, t1
rsq_pp r3.x, r2.x
dp3_pp r2.x, t2, t2
mul_pp r3.xyz, r3.x, t1
rsq_pp r2.x, r2.x
mad_pp r2.xyz, r2.x, t2, r3
dp3_pp r2.x, r2, r2
rsq_pp r2.x, r2.x
mul_pp r0.z, r2.x, r2
add r0.x, r0, -r1
mad_sat r3.x, v0.w, c3.z, c3.w
mad r0.x, r3, r0, r1
mov_pp r1.x, c2
max_pp r2.x, r0.z, c3
mul_pp r1.x, c3.y, r1
pow r4.x, r2.x, r1.x
add r1.x, v0, -r0
max_pp r2.x, r3.z, c3
mov_pp r3.xyz, c0
mad r1.x, v0.y, r1, r0
mov r0.x, r4.x
mul r0.x, r0, r1
mul_pp r1.xyz, r1.x, c0
mul_pp r2.xyz, r1, r2.x
cmp r1.x, -t3.z, c4.z, c4.w
mul_pp r1.x, r1, r0.w
mul_pp r1.x, r1, r5
mul_pp r3.xyz, c1, r3
mul_pp r1.x, r1, c5.y
mad r0.xyz, r3, r0.x, r2
mul r0.xyz, r0, r1.x
mov_pp r0.w, c3.x
mov_pp oC0, r0
"
}

{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;

  tmpvar_1.w = _glesTANGENT.w;

  tmpvar_5[1].y = tmpvar_4.y;
  tmpvar_5[1].z = tmpvar_2.y;
  tmpvar_5[2].x = tmpvar_3.z;
  tmpvar_5[2].y = tmpvar_4.z;
  tmpvar_5[2].z = tmpvar_2.z;

  v_6.y = _Object2World[1].x;
  v_6.z = _Object2World[2].x;

END

 // Stats for Vertex shader:
 //       d3d11 : 28 avg math (20..34)
 //    d3d11_9x : 28 avg math (20..34)
 //        d3d9 : 34 avg math (26..43)
 //      opengl : 33 avg math (25..42)
 // Stats for Fragment shader:
 //       d3d11 : 37 avg math (28..48), 3 avg texture (2..4)
 //    d3d11_9x : 37 avg math (28..48), 3 avg texture (2..4)
 //        d3d9 : 44 avg math (30..62), 3 avg texture (2..4)
 //      opengl : 41 avg math (28..56), 3 avg texture (2..4)
 Pass {
  Name "PREPASS"
  Tags { "LIGHTMODE"="PrePassFinal" }
  ZWrite Off
  Blend SrcAlpha OneMinusSrcAlpha
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 42 math
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_OFF" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_OFF" }
Bind "vertex" Vertex
Bind "color" Color
Bind "normal" Normal
Bind "texcoord" TexCoord0
Bind "tangent" ATTR14
Matrix 5 [_Object2World]
Matrix 9 [_World2Object]
Vector 13 [_WorldSpaceCameraPos]
Vector 14 [_ProjectionParams]
Vector 15 [unity_SHAr]
Vector 16 [unity_SHAg]
Vector 17 [unity_SHAb]
Vector 18 [unity_SHBr]
Vector 19 [unity_SHBg]
Vector 20 [unity_SHBb]
Vector 21 [unity_SHC]
Vector 22 [unity_Scale]
Vector 23 [_MainTex_ST]
"!!ARBvp1.0
PARAM c[24] = { { 1, 0.5 },
		state.matrix.mvp,
		program.local[5..23] };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
TEMP R3;
MUL R1.xyz, vertex.normal, c[22].w;
DP3 R2.w, R1, c[6];
DP3 R0.x, R1, c[5];
DP3 R0.z, R1, c[7];
MOV R0.y, R2.w;
MUL R1, R0.xyzz, R0.yzzx;
MOV R0.w, c[0].x;
DP4 R2.z, R0, c[17];
DP4 R2.y, R0, c[16];
DP4 R2.x, R0, c[15];
MUL R0.y, R2.w, R2.w;
DP4 R3.z, R1, c[20];
DP4 R3.x, R1, c[18];
DP4 R3.y, R1, c[19];
ADD R2.xyz, R2, R3;
MAD R0.w, R0.x, R0.x, -R0.y;
MUL R3.xyz, R0.w, c[21];
MOV R1.xyz, vertex.attrib[14];
MUL R0.xyz, vertex.normal.zxyw, R1.yzxw;
MAD R0.xyz, vertex.normal.yzxw, R1.zxyw, -R0;
MUL R0.xyz, R0, vertex.attrib[14].w;
MOV R1.xyz, c[13];
ADD result.texcoord[3].xyz, R2, R3;
MOV R1.w, c[0].x;
DP4 R0.w, vertex.position, c[4];
DP4 R2.z, R1, c[11];

SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }
"!!GLES


#ifdef VERTEX

attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord1;

uniform highp vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;

uniform highp mat4 _World2Object;

uniform highp vec4 unity_LightmapST;

varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying lowp vec4 xlv_COLOR0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD4;
void main ()
{

  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize(_glesTANGENT.xyz);
  tmpvar_1.w = _glesTANGENT.w;
  vec3 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = normalize(_glesNormal);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_3;

SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 25 math
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_ON" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }
Bind "vertex" Vertex
Bind "color" Color
Bind "normal" Normal
Bind "texcoord" TexCoord0
Bind "texcoord1" TexCoord1
Bind "tangent" ATTR14
Matrix 5 [_World2Object]
Vector 9 [_WorldSpaceCameraPos]
Vector 10 [_ProjectionParams]
Vector 11 [unity_Scale]
Vector 12 [unity_LightmapST]
Vector 13 [_MainTex_ST]
"!!ARBvp1.0
PARAM c[14] = { { 1, 0.5 },
		state.matrix.mvp,
		program.local[5..13] };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
MOV R0.xyz, vertex.attrib[14];
MUL R1.xyz, vertex.normal.zxyw, R0.yzxw;
MAD R0.xyz, vertex.normal.yzxw, R0.zxyw, -R1;
MUL R0.xyz, R0, vertex.attrib[14].w;
MOV R1.xyz, c[9];
MOV R1.w, c[0].x;
DP4 R0.w, vertex.position, c[4];
DP4 R2.z, R1, c[7];
DP4 R2.x, R1, c[5];
DP4 R2.y, R1, c[6];
MAD R2.xyz, R2, c[11].w, -vertex.position;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].y, R2, R0;
DP4 R0.z, vertex.position, c[3];
DP4 R0.x, vertex.position, c[1];
DP4 R0.y, vertex.position, c[2];
MUL R1.xyz, R0.xyww, c[0].y;
MUL R1.y, R1, c[10].x;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].z, vertex.normal, R2;
DP3 result.texcoord[1].x, R2, vertex.attrib[14];
ADD result.texcoord[2].xy, R1, R1.z;
MOV result.position, R0;
MOV result.color, vertex.color;
MOV result.texcoord[2].zw, R0;

TEX R3, fragment.texcoord[3], texture[3], 2D;
TEX R0, fragment.texcoord[0], texture[0], 2D;

MAD R2.w, R0.y, R2, R0.x;
ADD R0.y, R0.w, -R0.z;

LG2 R1.z, R1.z;

SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 28 math, 2 textures
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_OFF" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }
Vector 0 [_SpecColor]
Float 1 [_Opacity]
Float 2 [_RimFalloff]
Vector 3 [_RimColor]
SetTexture 0 [_MainTex] 2D 0
SetTexture 1 [_LightBuffer] 2D 1
"!!ARBfp1.0
PARAM c[5] = { program.local[0..3],
		{ 1, 3, 2 } };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
TEX R0, fragment.texcoord[0], texture[0], 2D;
TXP R1, fragment.texcoord[2], texture[1], 2D;
ADD R2.x, R0.y, -R0;
MUL_SAT R0.y, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4];
MAD R2.x, R0.y, R2, R0;
ADD R0.y, R0.w, -R0.z;
MAD_SAT R0.x, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4].y, -c[4].z;
MAD R0.x, R0, R0.y, R0.z;
ADD R0.y, R0.x, -R2.x;
MAD_SAT R0.x, fragment.color.primary.w, c[4].y, -c[4];
MAD R0.y, R0.x, R0, R2.x;
ADD R0.z, fragment.color.primary.x, -R0.y;
MAD R0.w, fragment.color.primary.y, R0.z, R0.y;
DP3 R0.x, fragment.texcoord[1], fragment.texcoord[1];
RSQ R0.x, R0.x;
MUL_SAT R0.x, R0, fragment.texcoord[1].z;
ADD R2.x, -R0, c[4];
ADD R1.xyz, R1, fragment.texcoord[3];
MUL R1.w, R0, R1;
MUL R0.xyz, R1, c[0];
POW R2.w, R2.x, c[2].x;
MUL R2.xyz, R0, R1.w;
MAD R1.xyz, R0.w, R1, R2;
MUL R0.xyz, R2.w, c[3];
MUL R0.xyz, R0, c[3].w;
MOV R0.w, c[1].x;
MAD result.color.xyz, R0, c[1].x, R1;
MAD result.color.w, R1, c[0], R0;
END
# 28 instructions, 3 R-regs
"
}
SubProgram "d3d9 " {
// Stats: 30 math, 2 textures
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_OFF" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }
Vector 0 [_SpecColor]
Float 1 [_Opacity]
Float 2 [_RimFalloff]
Vector 3 [_RimColor]
SetTexture 0 [_MainTex] 2D 0
SetTexture 1 [_LightBuffer] 2D 1
"ps_2_0
dcl_2d s0
dcl_2d s1
def c4, 1.00000000, 3.00000000, -1.00000000, -2.00000000
dcl t0.xy
dcl t1.xyz
dcl v0.xyzw
dcl t2
dcl t3.xyz
texld r2, t0, s0
texldp r3, t2, s1
add r1.x, r2.y, -r2
mul_sat r0.x, v0.w, c4.y
mad r0.x, r0, r1, r2
add r2.x, r2.w, -r2.z
mad_sat r1.x, v0.w, c4.y, c4.w
mad r1.x, r1, r2, r2.z
add r2.x, r1, -r0
mad_sat r1.x, v0.w, c4.y, c4.z
mad r1.x, r1, r2, r0
add r2.x, v0, -r1
dp3 r0.x, t1, t1
rsq r0.x, r0.x
mad r1.x, v0.y, r2, r1
mul_sat r0.z, r0.x, t1
mul_pp r0.x, r1, r3.w
add r2.x, -r0.z, c4
add_pp r4.xyz, r3, t3
pow_pp r3.x, r2.x, c2.x
mul_pp r2.xyz, r4, c0
mul_pp r2.xyz, r2, r0.x
mad_pp r4.xyz, r1.x, r4, r2
mov_pp r2.x, r3.x
mov_pp r1.x, c1
mad_pp r0.w, r0.x, c0, r1.x
mul r2.xyz, r2.x, c3
mul r0.xyz, r2, c3.w
mad_pp r0.xyz, r0, c1.x, r4
mov_pp oC0, r0
"
}

SubProgram "opengl " {
// Stats: 39 math, 4 textures
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }
Vector 0 [_SpecColor]
Float 1 [_Opacity]
Float 2 [_RimFalloff]
Vector 3 [_RimColor]
Vector 4 [unity_LightmapFade]
SetTexture 0 [_MainTex] 2D 0
SetTexture 1 [_LightBuffer] 2D 1
SetTexture 2 [unity_Lightmap] 2D 2
SetTexture 3 [unity_LightmapInd] 2D 3
"!!ARBfp1.0
PARAM c[6] = { program.local[0..4],
		{ 1, 3, 2, 8 } };
TEMP R0;
TEMP R1;
TEMP R2;
TEMP R3;
TEX R2, fragment.texcoord[3], texture[2], 2D;
TEX R3, fragment.texcoord[3], texture[3], 2D;
TEX R0, fragment.texcoord[0], texture[0], 2D;
TXP R1, fragment.texcoord[2], texture[1], 2D;
MUL R2.xyz, R2.w, R2;
DP4 R2.w, fragment.texcoord[4], fragment.texcoord[4];
MUL R3.xyz, R3.w, R3;
MUL R3.xyz, R3, c[5].w;
RSQ R2.w, R2.w;
RCP R2.w, R2.w;
MAD_SAT R2.w, R2, c[4].z, c[4];
MAD R2.xyz, R2, c[5].w, -R3;
MAD R2.xyz, R2.w, R2, R3;
ADD R1.xyz, R1, R2;
ADD R2.w, R0.y, -R0.x;
MUL_SAT R0.y, fragment.color.primary.w, c[5];
MAD R2.w, R0.y, R2, R0.x;
ADD R0.y, R0.w, -R0.z;
MAD_SAT R0.x, fragment.color.primary.w, c[5].y, -c[5].z;
MAD R0.x, R0, R0.y, R0.z;
ADD R0.z, R0.x, -R2.w;
DP3 R0.x, fragment.texcoord[1], fragment.texcoord[1];
MAD_SAT R0.y, fragment.color.primary.w, c[5], -c[5].x;
MAD R0.y, R0, R0.z, R2.w;
ADD R0.z, fragment.color.primary.x, -R0.y;
MAD R2.w, fragment.color.primary.y, R0.z, R0.y;
MUL R0.w, R2, R1;
MUL R2.xyz, R1, c[0];
RSQ R0.x, R0.x;
MUL_SAT R0.x, R0, fragment.texcoord[1].z;
ADD R0.x, -R0, c[5];
POW R0.x, R0.x, c[2].x;
MUL R2.xyz, R2, R0.w;
MUL R0.xyz, R0.x, c[3];
MOV R1.w, c[1].x;
MAD R1.xyz, R2.w, R1, R2;
MUL R0.xyz, R0, c[3].w;
MAD result.color.xyz, R0, c[1].x, R1;
MAD result.color.w, R0, c[0], R1;
END
# 39 instructions, 4 R-regs
"
}
SubProgram "d3d9 " {
// Stats: 39 math, 4 textures
Keywords { "LIGHTMAP_ON" "DIRLIGHTMAP_OFF" "HDR_LIGHT_PREPASS_ON" }

"ps_2_0

dcl_2d s1
dcl_2d s2

def c5, 1.00000000, 3.00000000, -1.00000000, -2.00000000
def c6, 8.00000000, 0, 0, 0
dcl t0.xy
dcl t1.xyz
dcl v0.xyzw
dcl t2
dcl t3.xy
dcl t4
texld r2, t0, s0
texldp r1, t2, s1
texld r0, t3, s2
texld r3, t3, s3
mul_pp r4.xyz, r0.w, r0
dp4 r0.x, t4, t4
mul_pp r3.xyz, r3.w, r3
mul_pp r3.xyz, r3, c6.x
rsq r0.x, r0.x
rcp r0.x, r0.x
mad_pp r4.xyz, r4, c6.x, -r3
mad_sat r0.x, r0, c4.z, c4.w
mad_pp r0.xyz, r0.x, r4, r3
add_pp r3.xyz, r1, r0
add r1.x, r2.y, -r2
mul_sat r0.x, v0.w, c5.y

add r2.x, r2.w, -r2.z
mad_sat r1.x, v0.w, c5.y, c5.w
mad r1.x, r1, r2, r2.z
add r5.x, r1, -r0
mad_sat r2.x, v0.w, c5.y, c5.z
mad r0.x, r2, r5, r0
dp3 r1.x, t1, t1
rsq r2.x, r1.x
mul_sat r0.z, r2.x, t1
add r2.x, -r0.z, c5
add r1.x, v0, -r0
mad r1.x, v0.y, r1, r0
pow_pp r5.x, r2.x, c2.x
mul_pp r0.x, r1, r1.w
mul_pp r4.xyz, r3, c0
mul_pp r2.xyz, r4, r0.x
mad_pp r3.xyz, r1.x, r3, r2
mov_pp r2.x, r5.x
mov_pp r1.x, c1
mad_pp r0.w, r0.x, c0, r1.x
mul r2.xyz, r2.x, c3
mul r0.xyz, r2, c3.w
mad_pp r0.xyz, r0, c1.x, r3

}
